                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="393">
                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="394">
                      Built as an elegant suite in the 1920's for the previous owners, this large room features a king bed, sitting area, large bathroom, stone fireplace, refrigerator, coffee maker, and a 'critter cam' to view the wildlife drinking from a water trough just outside the suite. It also features a private patio with table and chairs. The room is decorated with vintage prints and artwork from local artists.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="395">
                      Enchanting Trowbridge Suite A fascinating and enduring part of Arizona history, our original 1880s cattle-ranch was transformed into one of southern Arizona's earliest dude ranches and frequently hosted legendary Wild West showman “Buffalo Bill" Cody. With its lovely, whitewashed-adobe buildings, our property offers comfortable lodgings, privacy, easy-going hospitality, and the charm of a historic ranch setting. A delightful breakfast at the Main Ranch House's long, wooden kitchen table is available each morning to start your day. Bird-watching and wildlife viewing is an enjoyable pastime on our sprawling 50 acres. Enjoy contemporary art exhibited on the 6-acre Sculpture Park, a gift shop featuring locally-made crafts and fine art, as well as a gallery located in the historic Adobe Barn. The "Trowbridge Suite" is one large, light-filled room with king bed, a massive stone fireplace for romantic ambiance, a sitting area with twin daybed, walk-in closet, coffee maker and refrigerator, and a sunny bathroom with tub and shower. The unit opens up onto a shaded wildlife-viewing path and your own semi-private patio. Our most recently-added amenity is a 'Critter-Cam' filming live-action of our diverse wildlife. Besides a rich bird fauna, our property is home to deer, javelina, raccoons, foxes, bobcats and more. As natural as our property is, we are just a five minute drive to several popular eating establishments: one Old West themed steakhouse, one authentic Mexican family restaurant, a cosmopolitan breakfast &amp; lunch cafe/bistro, and two fine Italian restaurants. We are situated a mere 35 minutes from northwest Tucson and 5 minutes from Biosphere 2.
                     </div>

                      <li data-reactid="426"><p data-reactid="427">We really enjoyed our 2 night stay. We were visiting the Tucson area for a week and wanted to spend a couple of nights out of town in the country. So happy with our pick. Jim, the manager, couldn't have been more welcoming and was there to greet us and get us settled. His breakfasts were divine -- scrambled eggs delicately seasoned with lemon thyme, french toast and more. When my friend, mentioned she needed a massage, he suggested a great masseuse, Doug, who we were able to book an appointment with the next day, after a day of hiking, and he came to the room. The suite is roomy (with a nice seating area) and decorated with an eye towards comfort and beauty. The propane fireplace is very cozy in the evening. The only down side of the room was that the heater wasn't working properly, Jim took a look at it and tweaked it -- but it seems like it might be on it's last leg. They are looking into an upgrade, so if you're visiting at a cool time of year and like a bit of heat, I'd check to see if they've gotten to that. The ranch is funky and comfortable. Sharon, the owner has developed an amazing art walk in the desert landscape with outdoor sculpture -- we loved it best during the day when we could see all the details, but it's lit and meant to be walked at night, which is also fun. Given our delight with Jim's cooking, we asked if he could recommend a restaurant in Tuscon. His recommendation (Penca) was so yummy, we ate there twice. Our week long trip was all about being outside, hiking and looking at plants (both of us are serious gardeners, and I'm a horticulturist). Oracle State Park -- just minutes from the ranch was my favorite of all the parks we visited. Just blown away by the high desert landscape. I would certainly return to the Trowbridge suite -- Jim gave us a tour of the other 2 cottages and both were lovely. In warmer weather, I'd love to stay in the one with a sleeping porch -- or with a bigger group or extended visit there's a cabin with a kitchen. Also, both the Mexican and Italian (loved the ravioli, and Jim says the pizza is good too) restaurants in nearby Oracle were delicious -- the green chili tamales at the Mexican are light, fluffy and one more reason to return.</p><span data-reactid="428">Sarah</span><span data-reactid="429">2017-02-13T00:00:00Z</span></li>

I also include the hostel staff in this smorgasbord. I also used Couchsurfing some years ago, and I met a few marvelous people through it, but lately the site, and the people running it have messed up its system. AirBnB has taken the slack and created a new way to visit new places - and it has marvelous gems like Bill's place in Globe. It is up on a steep hill first off, from Yuma and Broad St., once you drive into downtown Globe. But Bill is sincere with everything. He explains how everything works, and offers most things in his little abode for you. Also, Bill introduced me to his neighbor, since I was a historian, and we even took a little hike to the Old Dominion Historic Mine Park. He also took me on a ride around his urban area showing me the place that I should visit. How many hosts would even do such things for their guests? Bill did all of that for me. I was also able to use his good kitchen to cook, and his low bed in my bedroom was great to sleep on. His wifi Internet was quite fast. We shared the small bathroom, but it was always clean and Bill gives enough towels for use. I even had a nasty fender bender in town, and Bill helped me out with that too when drove back to his place. Bill was such a great help and my friend in Globe. Thanks to Bill's integrity and company, my visit to Globe was not just a visit, it transformed into a wonderful experience. If I had stayed at a motel, or even a bed and breakfast, would I have experienced such a marvelous time? Definitely not, and I will for now on avoid such places, and avoid such visits - if there is no AirBnB or a hostel available. Thankfully, there is AirBnb that offers options for those in the traveling mode. And most thankfully, there are those wonderful hosts, such a Bill, that share not only their homes, but also their city - and even share their personal time and company. </p><span data-reactid="676">James</span><span data-reactid="677">2017-03-09T00:00:00Z</span></li>
                      <li data-reactid="678"><p data-reactid="679">Bill is a great host and I had a wonderful time there, he was incredibly helpful and except for my bad back on the futon it would have been perfect but other than that it was good!</p><span data-reactid="680">Stacey</span><span data-reactid="681">2017-03-22T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="780">
                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="781">
                      La Casita is located on 2.3 secluded acres adjacent to the Coronado National Forest. The house has a private, cozy ambiance, and a peaceful garden to relax in. Wild life and birds abound and the hiking trail head to Mt. Lemmon is just 5 minutes walk from the house. These features are what make the stay so special and enjoyable.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="782">
                      The house is surrounded by oak trees and native desert plants, it has a quiet, natural, atmosphere. Being adjacent to the National Forest wild life such as deer, javelinas, coyotes, bob cats, skunks, rabbits, and many types of birds can be seen often on the property. The house and garden are ideal for individuals or couples wanting a secluded, private environment to relax and revive in. Also it is excellent as a retreat or for concentrated work, there is excellent wifi. The rustic, 50 year old cottage of 750 sq. feet is furnished with many antiques from my family and original art. The house offers all that guests need to feel comfortable. There are sleeping arrangements for 4 persons, a double bed, and also a fold out couch that makes into a double bed. The screened-in porch provides an extra sitting area in the warmer months. A small but well equipped kitchen is perfect for cooking simple meals at home. The office area and a large table in the living room have comfortable office chairs and make great working areas for computer related or clean activities. Besides having great wifi, the house is LOW tech, there is a simple radio that receives NPR, and local stations, there is no TV. The beautiful garden and areas that surround the house are an important feature of La Casita. There are different sitting spaces that offer shade or sun and different views, they are perfect for eating and relaxing outside while watching the birds, or looking out at the Catalina Mountain foothills. Gorgeous sunsets can be seen from the house and at night the dark skies are perfect for stargazing. Upon Your Arrival You will be greeted by Chuck the care-taker who will give you the key, help you get settled, and answer any questions. The house is then yours to enjoy undisturbed on your own.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="783">
                      La Casita is located in the community of Oracle on the north sloops of the Catalina Mountains at 4800 ft. It is considered a High Desert eco system with its own unique combination of plant and animal species. Oracle is a cute little town, with many interesting and fun things to offer. There are several restaurants on American Avenue the main street. My favorites are the Patio Café for a really tasty breakfast or lunch and Rivera’s Mexican food, which has FABULOUS fish tacos on Fridays. The Oracle Inn is fun for a Friday or Saturday night, they often have live music and serve a good steak. The historic Arcadia Ranch Society is an interesting place to visit, it provides a unique view of the early frontier days of the area. If you like to explore a great vintage shop, be sure to visit The Ranch Store. They also offer on wednesday evenings the Farmer's Market with food and music, always a lot of fun. There is also the Oracle Post Office and Library. For general needs there is the Family General Store, but for food shopping the closest large grocery store and pharmacy is in Catalina about 20 min south of Oracle on the road to Tucson.
                     </div>

                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1053">
                      Private wing, with 2 Bedrooms, 1 Bath (2 sinks), and Laundry within an occupied foothills home. (Sofa Bedroom/exercise room is an additional fee of half price of full bdrm on that day.) Hone sits on quiet hill with East, West and South Mountain views on the North Side of Catalina Mountains foothills, 22 miles North of downtown Tucson, off Oracle Rd near Oro Valley. Tranquil water feature &amp; fire pit in rear. Great Outdoor kitchen &amp; living space. Gourmet Kitchen in home. Internet TV's/No Cable.
                     </div>

                      2 bedroom, 1 double sink bath, &amp; laundry in private wing of a split bedroom home. Price is 1 bdrm, 2nd bdrm has extra guest fee. Beautiful, tranquil patio with water feature, natural gas fire pit &amp; BBQ cooking center. Gourmet Kitchen in/out can be shared with homeowners.

                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="1900">
                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="1901">
                      Our spacious, sunny, comfortable studio with private entrance and bathroom, separated from the rest of the house, is a relaxing sanctuary in the middle of the city. It comfortably fits two &amp; is centrally located in a quiet, residential neighborhood just a few miles from the university and downtown, near a bus stop, bike path, park &amp; various restaurants. Enjoy carport parking, a private walkway/courtyard, beautifully tiled, fully equipped bathroom with walk-in shower, a mini fridge, coffee maker, tea kettle, as well as coffee, tea &amp; snacks. You'll also enjoy a shared back yard garden brimming with fruit trees, herbs &amp; flowers.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="1902">
                      We offer a large 450 sq feet studio with private entrance and private bathroom. Studio is not connected with the rest of the house. Studio is equipped with the queen size comfortable futon, with new bedding and high quality cotton sheets, comfortable butterfly chair with padded cushion and a foot ottoman, as well as a table with couple of chairs. There is no kitchen or cooking facilities, but there is a mini fridge, coffee maker, electric kettle, microwave, toaster, silverware and dishes available for you to use. We also provide a variety of teas, coffee, sugar and snacks. Private bathroom has a shower and is equipped with towels, shampoo, conditioner, soap, and necessary amenities, including a hair dryer. The large closet with shelves and hangers and plenty of room to store your stuff has a stereo connected with built in wall speakers you are welcome to use to play music from your phone or tablets. The studio has two entry doors. One leads to the covered carport with room for your car under it. You'll use a private walkway/courtyard with a small tiled bench and potted plants to reach the carport through the rustic metal gate. The other entry door will take you to the beautiful back yard/ garden area you'll share with us ( we live on the property). There are various sitting arrangements on the porches. You also are welcome to meditate or just relax and listen to birds singing in our hummingbird garden. We have a 2 year old lab named Onyx. He is a friendly indoor/outdoor dog who stays in the back yard sometimes (only when we are home). Please let us know if you are not fond or afraid of dogs so we can make sure Onyx doesn't disturb you. Note: there's no TV or cable in the studio, but there's internet and wifi.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="1903">
                      We live in a quiet, residential, very safe midtown neighborhood established in the first half of the 20th century in close proximity to amenities, parks, restaurants, shopping, university (3.5 miles) and downtown (4 miles). We are in walking distance or a short drive to Reed Park, the biggest park in Tucson, with a small, but very nicely designed zoo, well maintained rose garden, baseball fields, tennis courts, golf courses and an outdoor performance stage and of course walking and biking paths. We recommend visiting the ongoing Butterfly exhibit in the greenhouse of TheTucson Botanical Gardens, as well as the temporary Frida Kahlo art exhibit that ends May 31, 2017. These are very relaxing well established gardens right in the middle of the city, just a couple of miles from our house. There are a variety of restaurants within a mile or two: Polish cottage ( authentic Polish cuisine) Zayna ( Middle Eastern) Feast (eclectic cuisine with a menu that changes monthly) Guilin ( healthy Chinese) Lodge on the Desert Restaurant (fine, refined southwestern cuisine) a 10 min walk on neighborhood streets Bruegger's Bagels, Subway, and many more. Downtown, with its many great restaurants, art museum, theaters, convention center and of course Tucson Gem and Mineral Show is only 4 miles away accessible by bus (the bus stop is a 4 min walk). The closest gem show venue is only a mile away in The Double Tree Hotel.

The sectional in the living room is large enough to serve as an extra sleep space, and an additional twin-size air mattress can be provided upon request.

In our more direct vacinity, we have 2 cinemas (with a total of 7 screens), a bowling alley, and many eateries including; Mexican, Chinese, Steak Houses, and the usual array of Hamburger and Pizza joints. The Gila box is another great area to explore and only minutes away.

                    <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2280">
                     <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="2281">
                      Economy. There are 2 single size beds plus 1 single size stand alone day that each rent separately in shared room - share big house w amenities. Central locale near shopping &amp; UofA. Friendly conversation welcomed. Helpful owner lives and works here.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="2282">
                      This is an economy listing for saving money for short stays when needing a place to sleep, shower, change clothes and relax, rather than paying motel prices. What you can expect is an intent by the resident-owner-bachelor (Ron), to be friendly and helpful to you, while providing a fresh bed in a bunk room and use of the house common areas inside and out. Should not expect to find a professionally cleaned and maintained lodging house or hostel, and this listing is not intended for long term stays. You have use of the common areas in and around the house, and Ron is open to questions and conversation. The house is 2800 sq ft with 7 bedrooms; 3-4 are occupied by full-time adult single residents, including Ron; 1 room consists of an office; 1 room is the male bunk room; and 1 room is the female bunk room. Ron operates a small law practice inside the house. House is centrally located and convenient to main Tucson destinations.
                     </div>
                     <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="2283">
                      It is quiet, friendly, centrally located and convenient to essentials and popular locations.
                     </div>

When I arrived, he had a brisket going in his outdoor smoker, and everyone was invited to share his dinner. I watched some political coverage with Ron and shot hoops with his daughter.
